function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 293') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.293!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

// Dir added: doc
@mkdir('doc');
if (!is_dir('doc')) {
	warn('Directory could not be created: doc');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc', 0755)) {
	warn('Could not change directory permissions of doc');
}

if (is_file('userdata/info.txt') && (sha1_file('userdata/info.txt') != '4d71e5b79d19cc005a8f6f47f8c87faa0e76932b')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: userdata/info.txt');
	$tmp = pathinfo('userdata/info.txt');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('userdata/info.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('userdata/info.txt', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_18();
if (!is_file('userdata/info.txt')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): userdata/info.txt');
} else if (sha1_file('userdata/info.txt') != '4d71e5b79d19cc005a8f6f47f8c87faa0e76932b') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): userdata/info.txt');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('userdata/info.txt', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of userdata/info.txt');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_19();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '8456a1613c029e137fe3ca98cb10fd659780c0ae') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '8456a1613c029e137fe3ca98cb10fd659780c0ae') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'd45b3d0ab642926508be3320e7cf0bc486842012') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_19();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '8456a1613c029e137fe3ca98cb10fd659780c0ae') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
	writefile_20();
	if (!is_file('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php') != '09ab7f4677d264b7b30735999009d7931beece2c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php') !== '09ab7f4677d264b7b30735999009d7931beece2c') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php') !== '158acfbf78576e1f3185a4cd7df82218866c912d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_20();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php') !== '09ab7f4677d264b7b30735999009d7931beece2c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
		}
	}
}

	}

	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php') !== '6dfd9118ca52c6f9606912d36eba668dbacd2a6c') {

if (!is_file('includes/limits.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/limits.inc.php');
	writefile_26();
	if (!is_file('includes/limits.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/limits.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/limits.inc.php') != 'd6f0590a333277e8bd69f54b3904b626de1a63a7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/limits.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/limits.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/limits.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/limits.inc.php') !== 'd6f0590a333277e8bd69f54b3904b626de1a63a7') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/limits.inc.php') !== 'b128e7cb7c95a58c461e6b01f8a46fc9fb202b80') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/limits.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/limits.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/limits.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/limits.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_26();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/limits.inc.php') !== 'd6f0590a333277e8bd69f54b3904b626de1a63a7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/limits.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != 'af22e66e905efab7075ca1eaf42ca1a9660c8dbe') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');

		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');

			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_27();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'af22e66e905efab7075ca1eaf42ca1a9660c8dbe') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') != 'ed1020ee2599ca5067ff2eb154cc4c4e1e3fb31b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus_base.js', 0644)) {

	}

			if (!@copy('oidplus_base.js', $backup_name)) {

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	writefile_39();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') != 'f2f0e23e15e1ec1144ab72c941e975513f3fcde6') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== 'f2f0e23e15e1ec1144ab72c941e975513f3fcde6') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== 'e06986d0855739fc9441e4d2d26f8c4c08551a3c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_39();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== 'f2f0e23e15e1ec1144ab72c941e975513f3fcde6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/index.php');
	writefile_40();
	if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/index.php') != 'ff38ff9d441c725d5b249f7ee22477569fd7bf88') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== 'ff38ff9d441c725d5b249f7ee22477569fd7bf88') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== 'b0cecd74dd3649d2aa0d39302bb2ef86bc315287') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_40();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== 'ff38ff9d441c725d5b249f7ee22477569fd7bf88') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: update/index.php');
	writefile_44();
	if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/index.php') != '990dc12e85e1b2f4f3134a14e41dee702b0c3fee') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '990dc12e85e1b2f4f3134a14e41dee702b0c3fee') {
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== 'da153f4d4e5c798fd844ca0038d9b89b3c130d4e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('update/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_44();
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '990dc12e85e1b2f4f3134a14e41dee702b0c3fee') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('web.config')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: web.config');
	writefile_45();
	if (!is_file('web.config')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): web.config');
	} else if (sha1_file('web.config') != '855d479e3331e209525d301ac12eaf2f64d1f2c1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): web.config');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('web.config', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of web.config');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('web.config') !== '855d479e3331e209525d301ac12eaf2f64d1f2c1') {
		if (@sha1_file('web.config') !== 'd08e5510f96f888716704c520ece73bee10030f4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: web.config');
			$tmp = pathinfo('web.config');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('web.config')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('web.config', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_45();
		if (@sha1_file('web.config') !== '855d479e3331e209525d301ac12eaf2f64d1f2c1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): web.config');
		}
	}
}
